        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1103847797" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3186313335412760985"><br/> <b>Four Healing Stars!</b><br/><br/><br/>There were things I loved and things I really didn't like about this book. It's basically about three adult foster-brothers and their close bond, their scars, their battles in life after childhoods riddled with pain. Each brother gets his history and current story within this long book. That, however, was the reason for the deduction of a star. I felt I was in a maze and every chapter went in a different direction, but in the end, all the paths converge. <br/><br/><br/>Blake is a homeless m</span>
  <span id="freeText3186313335412760985" style="display:none"><br> <b>Four Healing Stars!</b><br><br><br>There were things I loved and things I really didn't like about this book. It's basically about three adult foster-brothers and their close bond, their scars, their battles in life after childhoods riddled with pain. Each brother gets his history and current story within this long book. That, however, was the reason for the deduction of a star. I felt I was in a maze and every chapter went in a different direction, but in the end, all the paths converge. <br><br><br>Blake is a homeless man, living in a train station. He suffers from delusions about an allergy to the sun, always remaining in the shadows. Livia passes by his "spot" everyday before and after work, always giving him a tender smile. She doesn't act like his not there, she notices him. He starts counting her smiles...<br><br><br><br><b>
  <i>"But when you saw me for the first time, you actually saw me. You saw me, and then you smiled like I was just the same as everyone else on that platform."</i>
</b><br><br><br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Used%20in%20review/556D842C-6960-4937-B444-65E3CDC62A04_zpsloinqagm.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1415969446i/11870349._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 556D842C-6960-4937-B444-65E3CDC62A04_zpsloinqagm.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br>Cole was dealt a very violent abusive childhood. He finds solace within the church. When offered a warm place to live, working as the church handyman, this appears to be a sign. He's on the path to becoming a priest...until he meets Kyle (Livia's sister). She's the other half of his soul. His path is now changed...<br><br><br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Used%20in%20review/00931AAF-B789-4BE7-AB74-1AD18AEB097A_zpsea63p6xa.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1415969446i/11870350._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 00931AAF-B789-4BE7-AB74-1AD18AEB097A_zpsea63p6xa.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br>Beckett, the protector of the three brothers, is anything but lawful. From the days he's spent enduring horrendous abuse in foster care so his brothers don't have to, he will do ANYTHING to keep them safe. The elusive, yet scary Eve is the one woman to crack his tough exterior, entering his heart, where no woman has gone before. <br><br><br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Used%20in%20review/116FC19F-9E57-4A9B-B000-7770D9C06776_zpsafedhhx7.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1415969446i/11870351._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 116FC19F-9E57-4A9B-B000-7770D9C06776_zpsafedhhx7.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br>***That's the premise to the series. Each man has battles to fight, love to win, happiness to be found. <br><br>I LOVED their brotherhood, their special tattoo, embrace, loyalty above all else. It broke my heart what they all went thru but quitting appears to be a no-go.<br><br>This book focuses most on Blake and Livia. He was such an endearing soul, she such a sweet heroine. Something about the man playing a fake piano keyboard on a piece of cardboard, his quirky gentleman behavior and speech draws her in. What's his story? How did he get here? How can she help his delusions of the sun harming his glass skin?<br><br>My biggest issue was the plethora of different routes the book went. This could easily be two books, almost three. I get the stories merge together but every single chapter went a different direction so I wanted to skip forward sometimes just to get resolution to the current story. <br><br>Cole and Kyle, well, that was insta-love at it's finest. Setting eyes one each other and bam, soul-mates. Not believable at all. I found myself thinking "Did they know each other before because no way can they meet and be professing their undying love, risking their lives for each other after one meeting."<br><br>Sometimes the humor within the book was...off for me. Like it didn't fit the character or the scene. Both Beckett and Kyle are the comedians in the book. <br><br>Looking forward to more about Beckett. He's the true anti-hero that the reader can't help but love. The other characters have some resolution within this book so I'm hoping Beckett is next...<br><br> </span>
  <a data-text-id="3186313335412760985" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_245303278" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/245303278" />
    <a title="Duchess Nicole" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2204947-duchess-nicole"><img alt="Duchess Nicole" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1499265843p2/2204947.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/245303278?book_show_action=true">Dec 10, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Duchess Nicole" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Duchess Nicole" href="/user/show/2204947-duchess-nicole">Duchess Nicole</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=read-in-2012">read-in-2012</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=e-pcs">e-pcs</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=genre-contemp-romance">genre-contemp-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=genre-ya">genre-ya</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer245303278" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15019919540191345845">Let me start by saying that this book was not at all what I thought it would be. I expected a sappy love story, and had no problem with that. But the story evolves into a truly gripping tale of family, love and acceptance. More than anything, it brings to light that the choices you make - the choice to ridicule or bully, or the choice to turn away in apathy, may not seem huge to you. But your smile could mean so much to someone who is normally overlooked. And a helping hand could change lives.<br/><br/>Fo</span>
  <span id="freeText15019919540191345845" style="display:none">Let me start by saying that this book was not at all what I thought it would be. I expected a sappy love story, and had no problem with that. But the story evolves into a truly gripping tale of family, love and acceptance. More than anything, it brings to light that the choices you make - the choice to ridicule or bully, or the choice to turn away in apathy, may not seem huge to you. But your smile could mean so much to someone who is normally overlooked. And a helping hand could change lives.<br /><br />For the first 100 pages or so, I was a bit disappointed. I felt as if the writing was juvenile, and the story was just weird. I mean, here's this homeless guy who falls in love with a girl just because she smiles at him? And she starts to fall for him, too!? There are a few scenes that seemed like a high school drama written on paper. But then...oh, then...<br /><br />More players are introduced to the storyline. At first, you don't realize how much they will come to mean to you as a reader. Beckett and Cole are Blake's foster brothers from their parent-less days in the system. These boys have formed a bond nearly stronger than family. After all, you can't choose family. But they chose each other, although they are all three so very different. Through the years, their bond has become even stronger.<br /><br />Livia has noticed Blake at the Poughkeepsie train station for quite some time. She's a happy woman, and also kind and caring. She doesn't realize that each time she smiles at him, he's counting those smiles, storing them up even though he's never dreamed of having more from her. One day, the two finally meet when Livia overhears some punk teenagers planning on shaming the faceless homeless man. From there, it's as if every day of their lives was lived only so the two of them would meet. <br /><br />While Livia and Blake's story is the headliner, there are so many other things going on behind the scenes. Love and lust, betrayal and utter loyalty, but above all, life, and not only the utter beauty of having the ability to make your own choices but the power of affecting the choices of others. This is a story of such an unlikely group of young people, thrown together because of the love of two of them. It's so chaotic, but it also makes sense. And it proves that not all of the bad guys are all bad. Some of them just have tough choices to make.<br /><br />*********************************<br />Please, PLEASE tell me there is a sequel to this! While the story of Blake and Livia feels resolved, there is another that left me aching. Any who have finished it knows who I mean. And I just hope so badly that the author plans to finish that story. Even a tiny novella? He/she deserves it!<br /><br />EDIT:<br />What a ramble! I just reread my review. It doesn't even make sense to me! I'll just say this: I will remember this book. After two hundred more book plots and couples get in the way, I know I'll remember this story. It's extremely original, and an unexpected tearjerker. Beautiful story, even if you don't agree with decisions made by the characters.</span>
  <a data-text-id="15019919540191345845" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_293056906" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/293056906" />
    <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie"><img alt="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514769932p2/3275325.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/293056906?book_show_action=true">Mar 12, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie">Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781936305957" href="/book/show/13110316-poughkeepsie">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=emotional-angsty-books">emotional-angsty-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=read-in-2012">read-in-2012</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer293056906" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4365546492406610012">**4.5 stars**<br/><br/>Livia takes the train to work every day and smiles at everyone...even the homeless guy. One day, he is being bullied and Livia steps up to help him and her life changes from that moment on. <br/><br/>Wow...this book is sooo much more that I thought it would be and sooo different. Yes, it is a love story with a homeless guy but you have to give it a chance. It will be worth it. <br/><br/>Blake is sweet and kind and romantic but he has some problems. It's a bit scary for Livia but she follows her heart e</span>
  <span id="freeText4365546492406610012" style="display:none">**4.5 stars**<br /><br />Livia takes the train to work every day and smiles at everyone...even the homeless guy. One day, he is being bullied and Livia steps up to help him and her life changes from that moment on. <br /><br />Wow...this book is sooo much more that I thought it would be and sooo different. Yes, it is a love story with a homeless guy but you have to give it a chance. It will be worth it. <br /><br />Blake is sweet and kind and romantic but he has some problems. It's a bit scary for Livia but she follows her heart even though she has a police officer Dad. She is also tempted to help him since she is studying psychology but basically she just wants to because deep down she has already fallen for him and now just has to accept it. <br /><br />Like I said, there is sooo much more going on than just a love story between Blake and Livia. We have a horrible relationship with a soon to be ex-boyfriend, Livia's wonderful relationship with her sister, Kyle and her Dad, Blake's relationships with his brothers, Cole and Beckett, Beckett's relationship with Mouse, Beckett's relationship with Eve, Eve's relationship with Blake, and Cole's relationship with Kyle. And that's not everything! <br /><br />I loved the relationship with the brothers and their tattoos. It was so great how they were there for each other and just fit so well together. (The part where Beckett had to watch and not participate killed me.) <br /><br />But there were a few things that bothered me. The first time in the meadow freaked me out...it actually made me feel a bit sick. I thought there would be no hope. It was great how Livia helped Blake but I wanted to know more and it seemed that he got "fixed" too easily. And I wanted to know <i>exactly</i> why he was homeless all that time. Also, Beckett was a bit too extreme. Well, he is too extreme in almost everything but I felt the killings were too much. <br /><br />I liked how everything wrapped up. In fact, I was going to complain that things got wrapped up too nicely so I'm glad that she left one thing undone. I've heard that a Beckett and Eve book is in the works and that makes me very happy! ((Thanks Rhonda)) <br /><br />Favorite quotes: <br /><br />♥ “Don’t put off happiness you can have today. Tomorrow is a hope, not a promise.” <br /><br />♦ “Remember when you and Livia tried to hog the spotlight at my wedding? Just when you and Livia get to the good part, Cole and I are going to have porno sex right there.” ((love Kyle))<br /><br />♥ And I will never, ever lose count. ((my favorite part is counting the smiles))<br /><br /><br /><br />**Also there is a great book trailer that you shouldn't miss: <br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=3tHdSFrxnp4">http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=3tHdSF...</a><br /><br /><br /><br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="4365546492406610012" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('LUKG5lkqnDXo5CB8uNVR613ztYITtAjEyXk7tspBwrv4O2Ne7YWnaSmuDqfu/dtUOgCgR9XFOj81M7k8aRjcxQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('vtNTBzsd/BjQrJfIYdJ0QaRU+W8YY72vCivOHOpAhVdrqra/j7LHRBHmuRM3+v7+w6fsqt4Sj1T2YUyWSRmbKQ==')})
  }

His calling, his craft are destruction and intimidation—whether he wants it that way now or not. He left Poughkeepsie to keep his brothers safe, to keep Eve safe. Set up with happy lives to live, they’re better off without him, right?\n\nBut all his willpower crumbles when he hears his brother Blake’s frantic voice on the phone. An unknown enemy has moved in on his old territory, and Livia’s been taken. In an instant, Beckett knows it will take an attack only he and Eve can execute to bring her back. All his self-imposed embargoes are torn to shreds, perhaps along with the new man he’s struggled to become.\n\n“Brother, call Eve. I’ll be there soon.” \n\nIn this emotional and action-packed sequel to Poughkeepsie, Debra Anastasia conjures a tale of love at its most raw and ragged. With Beckett and Eve, how could we expect anything less? But even when it’s messy, not magical, true love perseveres.
